### 1204112361380651068
## (ʘɤʘ) (einowl) 02/05/2024 17:12 

> A730 (legion y90 16ram) gmem driver test.
> skyline 69 (same result with R17 KGSL+a750):
> diablo 3 - freeze on loading
> crash bandicoot 4 - don't start
> luigi's mansion 3 - half textures on loading and closing game
> mario rabbids kingdom - don't start
> mario cart 8 - don't start
> mario 3d world - black background and closing game after some seconds
> bowser fury - black triangles flickering in the sky with 20-25fps and closing game after some seconds
> link's awakening - 15-20fps and texture bug with spark effects from hitting etc
> valkyria chronicles 4 - closing game after loading a mission
> 
> yuzu 212 (latest stable for me):
> diablo 3 - freeze right after appearing in town
> crash bandicoot 4 - after loading level, has 1 second of gameplay and freeze with closing
> luigi's mansion 3 - it work's fine (x1 has same texture bug like on other turnips, so x0.75+ddr mod for stable fps), but game closing after
> changing location
> mario rabbids kingdom - has same shadow/light issue and closing game after some seconds of gameplay
> mario kart 8 - game closing in race after 1 2 3 start
> mario 3d world - freeze after some seconds before main menu appering
> bowser fury - closing game after 1 minute of gameplay
> link's awakening - 15-20 fps and closing game after changing location, with nce it's same+some more fps+texture flickering
> valkyria chronicles 4 - closing game after loading a mission
> 
> for now, r17+a750 is best driver for me and 757 driver for valkyria chronicles 4.

### 1212911274988540004
### [Replying to 1212881731518988309](#1212881731518988309)
## KIMCHI (omnisoju) 02/29/2024 23:56 

> While Turnip can be used for emulation, its primary purpose isn't there. It functions just like a traditional PC GPU driver, managing the graphics processing unit on your Android device. That's basically it.
> Beyond emulation, the Android modding community embraces Turnip as its primary driver for several reasons. Firstly, some prop drivers remain buggy, hindering basic functions and gaming. Secondly, Turnip can offer performance improvements in certain cases. However, the emulation scene likely boasts the largest user base for Turnip.
> 
> Btw, I dont think cassia, winlator and the others count as emulation since they're compatibility layers. Theyre not involved in reverse engineering tpm's or translating console code languages. Support will continue for them.

## Versalhes (versalhes.) 03/02/2024 04:45 

> Just to confirm, the most recent version on your github is always the best, right?

### 1213349377909858305
## Moonlacer (moonlacer) 03/02/2024 04:57 

> That's not really how it works in the driver world 😅 
> Latest does not always mean greatest. Sometimes newer drivers will perform better or have less graphical issues than older versions, but may also introduce regressions in those same ways
> This is why other driver options are good to have, and the driver management tool now built-in to yuzu makes this much easier
